mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、马纳普汗（哈萨克）、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">马淑芬、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">马义涛、马玉凤、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">马月琴</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">麦尔丹•赛伊塔洪（维吾尔）、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">买麦提明•买吐松（哈萨克）、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">买买提江•阿布都拉（维吾尔）、</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">曼嘎（藏）</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">毛德君</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">米久平、米玛顿珠（藏）、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">明经国、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">孟庆素、孟宪强、孟晓东、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">莫伟秋、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">牟永霞</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">穆塔力浦•伊明（维吾尔）、木拉提别克．吾麻尔（哈）、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">马宝玲<span lang="EN-US">: </span></span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">江苏省连云港市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日，连云港市海州区公安分局抓捕了法轮功学员刘玉萍、邵世玲、那仁志、熊成霞、周翠萍、马宝玲、高建君、王艾芝、汪宝玉、小周女士、乔老太等十一人。所有人家中都被非法抄了家，警察劫走家中的电脑、手机、光盘、<span lang="EN-US">U</span>盘、电器、钱财、书籍等私人物品。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，马宝玲被开庭，被判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><a name="_Hlk52181848"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">马凤菊：</span></b></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk52181848;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">辽宁省清原县法轮功学员。</span></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2019</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，马凤菊、刘玉英在清原易和小区发放法轮功资料，被清原镇河南派出所警察王东等人抓捕，被关押在抚顺看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日开庭，未当庭宣判。后获悉，<a name="_Hlk52326462">马凤菊</a>被判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，刘玉英被判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">马纳普汗（哈萨克）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">新疆阿尔泰地区哈萨克族居民，哈萨克族良心犯、人权捍卫者。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月，因其获得一本从哈萨克斯坦国带回的《古兰经》，所以被当地公安局将其一家三口悉数抓走，并被指控“持有非法宗教出版物”。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月，其“持古兰经案”被当地法院开庭审理，一家三口分别被以“持有非法宗教出版物罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年。开庭前，其要求聘请律师遭拒。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">马淑芬：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">天津市河北区法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">1944</span>年生，退休教师，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月，被检察院、法院构陷，准备对她判刑。法院以岁数大可以从轻处理，但是不放弃炼法轮功，就严判为条件，企图让<a name="_Hlk52326546">马淑芬</a>放弃修炼法轮功，马淑芬拒绝。在<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月中旬，马淑芬被判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。在天津女子监狱服刑。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">马义涛：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">黑龙江省北安市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日夜晚，马义涛等三名法轮功学员开车到五大连池市发放法轮功真相资料。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日凌晨，他们被跟踪的警察抓捕，同时被抓捕的法轮功学员还有李学良、盛春霞。随后警察驱车到北安市城区马义涛的家抄家，抢劫走几本大法著作和真相资料，并抓捕了马义涛的妻子马英杰。）<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，马义涛等四人被黑龙江省亚布力林区法院判刑。马义涛被判<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年，李学良<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，马英杰<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，盛春霞判三年缓四年，已回家。马义涛、李学良不服法院非法判决，提出上诉。马义涛刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 351.75pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">马玉凤：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">江苏省镇江市润州区维权人士。因为在<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年清明时，到北京福田公墓祭奠杨佳，在“十一”维稳时，被公安以“涉嫌寻衅滋事罪”指定监视居住。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年的最后一天，马玉凤直接由指定监视居住转为批捕。目前无具体信息。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><a name="_Hlk55008952"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">马月琴</span></b></a><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">河南省漯河市临颖县退休女教师、法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">1950</span>年代生人。马月琴</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2019</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">11</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">月</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">29</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">日去临颖县杜曲镇面对面发法轮功台历时被抓捕，关押在漯河市第二看守所，经查证，</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2020</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">7-8</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">月间被临颖法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年半。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">玛乌提•么斯尔汗（哈萨克）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">他与</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">纳杂尔﹒叶尔江、哈纳提别克﹒萨布尔别克、阿尔恒﹒巴杂尔别克、乌木别提﹒卡斯木、哈伊拉提别克﹒木合塔尔汗、沙部旦﹒沙伊合、耶尔肯别克﹒达列力、肯杰别克﹒达列力都是新疆伊利市哈萨克自治州阿尔泰市巴里巴盖乡人，哈萨克族，穆斯林。其中，纳杂尔﹒叶尔江<span lang="EN-US">26</span>岁，哈纳提别克﹒萨布尔别克<span lang="EN-US">26</span>岁，阿尔恒﹒巴杂尔别克<span lang="EN-US">27</span>岁，乌木别提﹒卡斯木<span lang="EN-US">31</span>岁，哈伊拉提别克﹒木合塔尔汗<span lang="EN-US">37</span>岁，沙部旦﹒沙伊合约<span lang="EN-US">30</span>岁，耶尔肯别克﹒达列力<span lang="EN-US">30</span>岁，肯杰别克﹒达列力<span lang="EN-US">27</span>岁，玛乌提﹒么斯尔汗约<span lang="EN-US">30</span>岁。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">-8</span>月，因他们分别在私下里进行了穆斯林传统常规祷告仪式，而被中共新疆伊犁市哈萨克自治州阿尔泰当局知晓后拘捕，遂很快被阿尔泰市地方法院以“非法从事宗教活动”和“从事宗教极端活动”为由分别判处<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">-6</span>年不等刑期。目前各人具体判刑不详，刑至日期不详，服刑监狱不详，服刑状况及健康程度等不详。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">麦尔丹•赛伊塔洪（维吾尔）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">新疆维吾尔自治区伊犁哈萨克族自治州伊宁县人，因笃信伊斯兰教，同时又经常收留流落街头的儿童，宣传和教育他们学做好人、遵守宗教道德，从而碰触到当局的敏感神经；又因中共长期以来对维吾尔人的宗教信仰采取高压控制政策（中共当局相关法规规定，凡私自进行宗教信仰教育属违法行为，凡私自指导、主持伊斯兰教教育属从事“非法”宗教活动），不仅对进出清真寺的人员实施全面监控，而且对<span lang="EN-US">18</span>岁以下维吾尔青少年、维吾尔共产党员进寺礼拜更是予以极力限制，尤其是明令禁止跨村礼拜，限制朝觐，严禁穿“伊斯兰”服饰，禁止学生及公务员按宗教教义习俗封斋等，故而在<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月—<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月的新疆地区宗教活动大抓捕行动中，在伊犁哈萨克族自治州伊宁县和尼勒克县竟抓捕了<span lang="EN-US">12</span>名伊斯兰教宣传者；在此高压管控下，<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日<span lang="EN-US">,</span>其亦被伊宁市警方以涉嫌“分裂国家罪”刑拘，并被指控有向青少年灌输“非法”宗教的行为，属从事以“分裂主义”为目的的非法宗教活动，是“分裂分子”，后被以同罪名正式逮捕；<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日被新疆维吾尔自治区伊犁中级法院以“分裂国家罪”秘密判处无期徒刑；其代理律师被政府指定。目前在新疆维吾尔自治区伊犁哈萨克族自治州伊宁县监狱服刑。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">买麦提明﹒买吐松（哈萨克）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">新疆和田市伊里其乡嘎宗村农民，伊斯兰教信仰者。因经常使用穆斯林祷告方式，被当地公安局认为参与了“非法宗教活动”，<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月，被新疆和田市中级法院以“从事非法宗教活动罪”判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。目前羁押于新疆和田市看守所。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4-5</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">买买提江•阿布都拉（维吾尔）</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">：<span lang="EN-US">1977</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日出生，新疆维吾尔自治区克拉玛依人，原中央人民广播电台维语部播音员、记者、编辑，业余担任维语彩丽肯（清风）网（<span lang="EN-US">salkin.cn</span>）主持人，独立中文笔会荣誉会员，中国在押政治犯、良心犯。<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年因广东韶关<span lang="EN-US">6</span>•<span lang="EN-US">26</span>事件后接受境外记者采访，把世界维吾尔大会发言人的示威号召等一些汉语敏感文章翻译成维语，发表在中国境内维语网站彩丽肯网（<span lang="EN-US">salkin.cn</span>），有协助煽动之后乌鲁木齐<span lang="EN-US">7</span>•<span lang="EN-US">5</span>事件的嫌疑，遂于<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月被警方逮捕；<span lang="EN-US">2010</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，买买提江•阿布都拉被新疆乌鲁木齐市中级人民法院以“分裂国家、泄露国家秘密和组织非法示威罪”判处无期徒刑。目前在新疆维吾尔自治区伊犁哈萨克自治州塔城的乌苏监狱服刑。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">曼嘎：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">女，四川省甘孜藏族羌族自治区州阿坝县麦尔玛乡藏人，父亲名叫次培，母亲叫白玛吉。麦尔玛乡在过去一年中曾发生多起独自游街抗议中共暴政的活动。<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年中共当局在麦尔玛乡境内强迫每户藏人家庭悬挂中共五星红旗，当时曼嘎不但拒绝这一无理要求，并与官方人员争辩，结果被非法关押<span lang="EN-US">8</span>个多月，其间遭受了折磨虐待。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日中午<span lang="EN-US">12</span>点左右，曼嘎在麦尔玛乡一处街道上独自开展了示威活动，当时曼嘎双手举着达赖喇嘛尊者的法像，并呼喊出口号，中共公安随即赶到现场将她拘捕。后音信全无。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">毛德君：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1954</span>年生，山东莒南县，法轮功学员，东北某中学退休物理教师。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日，莒南县警察抓捕了法轮功学员毛德君。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，在北京维权律师做出无罪辩护情况下，山东省临沂市临沭县法院法官吴淑芳，对莒南县法轮功学员毛德君女士，枉法判决<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 351.75pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">米久平：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">深圳佳士工人。因要求组建独立工会，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日被深圳警方以寻衅滋事罪刑事拘留，同时被刑事拘留的有<span lang="EN-US">14</span>名工人。关押在深圳龙岗区看守所。已关押两年多，未有案件进展信息。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">米玛顿珠（藏）：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">1973</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">年出生，西藏自治区日喀则定日县人，藏名<span lang="EN-US">Migmar Dhondup</span>，社会工作者，中国在押政治犯。曾于<span lang="EN-US">1990</span>年代中期在南印度某学院研读商务课程，后返回西藏，致力于为百姓谋福利，在山南和拉萨地区，与当地农民和牧民一起努力改善卫生条件，规划社会发展计划，并呼吁西方人支持和参与这些计划；<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月，因在拉萨市<span lang="EN-US">3</span>•<span lang="EN-US">14</span>事件中参与和平抗议活动而被当局逮捕，同年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，又以“接受西藏流亡政府指派，在拉萨建立地下情报网络，大量复制并散发具有煽动分裂国家内容的光盘和煽动‘举行西藏人民大起义运动’的传单，以及给境外收集涉及国家安全和利益的情报”等为由，被拉萨市中级法院以“间谍罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">14</span>年，剥夺政治权利<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。 目前在西藏自治区拉萨市曲水监狱服刑。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 351.75pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">明经国：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">江西赣州南康乡<span lang="EN-US">6</span>旬农民明经国反强拆锄杀官员案。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日上午，该乡人大主席卓宇和村干部多人再次来到村民明经国家，强拆明经国祖屋，遭反抗。卓宇被明经国用镰铲击伤，因伤势过重送医后死亡。<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日上午，明经国被捕，后被刑事拘留，<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日开庭审理，开庭未判。</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">江西反强拆明经国“锄死”乡干部案<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日宣判，明经国被赣州中院以故意杀人罪一审判处死刑，缓期<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年执行，剥夺政治权利终身。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">孟庆素：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">四川省成都市人，成都市双流区西航港莲花小区居民，法轮功信仰者、良心犯。因信仰、宣传法轮功，<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日被成都市公安局天府新区分局警方非法绑架，并于<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日在成都市双流区法院非法开庭。在庭上，尽管其拒绝认罪，且其辩护律师认为该案所列证据不足以作为定罪依据，被告人的行为不构成犯罪，但最终仍被该法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">孟宪强：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">山东潍坊市昌乐县法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日下午，昌乐县红河镇法轮功学员孟宪强被红河镇派出所警察非法抄家并绑架。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日被山东青州法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">.</span>刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5 </span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">孟晓东：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">（身份证名字孟跟东<span lang="EN-US">)</span>河南商丘睢县人，<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年因村里土地问题走上维权之路。孟晓东经常参加公益活动，如参与过河南反平坟、为河南许昌被强拆户李建国呼吁等维权活动。曾在于世文、陈卫夫妇发起的六四公祭有签名。因维权多次被抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日，孟晓东被河南睢县公安局以涉嫌寻衅滋事罪刑事拘留，现羁押于河南商丘睢县看守所。随后被批准逮捕。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月底开庭，尚未判决。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">莫伟秋：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">天津市宁河区法轮功学员天津市宁河区廉庄乡廉庄村人，与丈夫李广远于一九九七年开始修炼法轮功。自<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年以来，夫妇俩多次被中共非法关押、劳教并被非法判刑，在被非法审判和监禁期间，夫妇俩多次遭到毒打和酷刑折磨。莫伟秋因控告江泽民，于<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日被绑架，再次被判<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年半。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">牟永霞：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1948</span>年生，大庆市退休教师、法轮功学员。因坚持修炼法轮功，<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日深夜被抓捕，被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，在黑龙江省女子监狱遭受迫害，被折磨得身体极度衰弱，手脚麻木，经常头晕。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日牟永霞被哈尔滨市铁路公安处便衣警察抓捕抄家。牟永霞老人被关押在哈尔滨市第二看守所，绝食抗议抓捕、关押，身体状况被迫害得虚弱，看守所强行给<span lang="EN-US">72</span>岁的牟永霞老人灌食、灌药，进行人身及精神折磨。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月牟永霞老人被大庆市法院判<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">穆塔力浦•伊明（维吾尔）：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">1988</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日出生，新疆维吾尔自治区和田市洛浦县人，维吾尔族名<span lang="EN-US">Mtuellip<span style="mso-spacerun: yes;">&nbsp; </span>Imin</span>，原中央民族大学英语专业本科毕业生，土耳其伊斯坦布尔大学社会学在读硕士留学生，中国在押政治犯。曾于<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年在中央民族大学攻读英语翻译专业，<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月毕业后又成功申请到土耳其国家奖学金项目（<span lang="EN-US">Turkish Scholarships</span>），遂于<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月前往土耳其伊斯坦布尔大学留学，攻读土耳其语（第一年）和社会学硕士（后两年）；<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月初回国度假；但当其于<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日再度前往土耳其继续求学时，在北京首都机场遭到警方拦截，被新疆维吾尔自治区公安厅非法关押<span lang="EN-US">79</span>天，并被胁迫强行修改口供，否则会被“依法判刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>—<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年”；<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日获释后，其计算机、电话、护照及身份证等重要物品仍被新疆警方扣留，致使根本其无法离境求学；无奈之下，其多次上网维权，并举牌要求新疆警方归还所扣之物，且能准予出境继续留学。<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，其在中央民族大学时期的老师、维族学者伊力哈木•土赫提被新疆警方拘捕，其亦于当日被新疆自治区和田市洛浦县警方从家中带走，被以涉嫌“分裂国家罪”刑事拘留；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，因其案件被定为“分裂国家犯罪集团案”而被乌鲁木齐市检察院正式批捕；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，其案件在乌鲁木齐巿中级法院开庭审理；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，被乌鲁木齐巿中级法院以“积极参与分裂国家犯罪集团罪”重判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">3-8</span>年，最多将于<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日出狱。服刑监狱不详。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">木拉提别克．吾麻尔（哈）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">新疆伊犁哈萨克自治州巩留县吉尔格郎乡阿勒玛勒村清真寺教长助手。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，在参加哈萨克族传统节日纳乌鲁斯节后被捕，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月获悉被判刑<span lang="EN-US">18</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2036</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 22.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">N.<o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">纳杂尔•叶尔江（哈萨克）、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">那仁志、<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">南杰顿珠（藏）、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">倪会仙</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">聂广丰、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">聂丽娜、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">宁惠荣、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">牛占华、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">努尔哈因﹒木哈麦提沙尔（哈萨克）、<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">努尔兰（哈萨克）、<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">纳杂尔﹒叶尔江：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">他与哈纳提别克﹒萨布尔别克、阿尔恒﹒巴杂尔别克、乌木别提﹒卡斯木、哈伊拉提别克﹒木合塔尔汗、沙部旦﹒沙伊合、耶尔肯别克﹒达列力、肯杰别克﹒达列力、玛乌提﹒么斯尔汗都是新疆伊利市哈萨克自治州阿尔泰市巴里巴盖乡人，哈萨克族，穆斯林。其中，纳杂尔﹒叶尔江<span lang="EN-US">26</span>岁，哈纳提别克﹒萨布尔别克<span lang="EN-US">26</span>岁，阿尔恒﹒巴杂尔别克<span lang="EN-US">27</span>岁，乌木别提﹒卡斯木<span lang="EN-US">31</span>岁，哈伊拉提别克﹒木合塔尔汗<span lang="EN-US">37</span>岁，沙部旦﹒沙伊合约<span lang="EN-US">30</span>岁，耶尔肯别克﹒达列力<span lang="EN-US">30</span>岁，肯杰别克﹒达列力<span lang="EN-US">27</span>岁，玛乌提﹒么斯尔汗约<span lang="EN-US">30</span>岁。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">-8</span>月，因他们分别在私下里进行了穆斯林传统常规祷告仪式，而被中共新疆伊犁市哈萨克自治州阿尔泰当局知晓后拘捕，遂很快被阿尔泰市地方法院以“非法从事宗教活动”和“从事宗教极端活动”为由分别判处<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">-6</span>年不等刑期。目前各人具体判刑不详，刑至日期不详，服刑监狱不详，服刑状况及健康程度等不详。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">那仁志：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">江苏省连云港市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日，连云港市海州区公安分局抓捕了法轮功学员刘玉萍、邵世玲、那仁志、熊成霞、周翠萍、马宝玲、高建君、王艾芝、汪宝玉、小周女士、乔老太等十一人。所有人家中都被非法抄了家，警察劫走家中的电脑、手机、光盘、<span lang="EN-US">U</span>盘、电器、钱财、书籍等私人物品。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，那仁志被开庭，被判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">南杰顿珠（藏）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">出生年月不详，四川省甘孜藏族自治州炉霍县人，炉霍寺僧人，中国在押良心犯。由于中共当局在西藏及其周边各省涉藏地区强硬推行“爱国和法制宣传教育”活动，引发多地藏民强烈不满，四川省甘孜州炉霍县藏民于<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日（即当年中国农历新年初一）举行大规模和平示威活动；该活动立即惨遭当地警方严厉的武力镇压和任意抓捕，致使上百藏人被抓，多人被打死打伤；至同年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，共有<span lang="EN-US">36</span>人被中共当局判处<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>个月直至无期徒刑不等的刑期，另有数人被捕后完全失踪；南杰顿珠亦因积极参与抗议示威游行，于<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月被警方以“参与和带头示威活动”为由从当地炉霍寺抓走刑拘；<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，被甘孜藏族自治州炉霍县法院以“炉火示威活动的主要带头人”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">14</span>年。目前在四川省甘孜藏族自治州康定县监狱服刑。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">倪会仙</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：昆明法轮功学员。女，<span lang="EN-US">1952</span>年生。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月法轮功学员杨靖波、武存仙、<a name="_Hlk52327447">倪会仙</a>由于在小区粘贴「法轮大法好！真善忍好！」不干胶，和向住户赠送「天赐洪福」法轮功小册子，被安宁市金方街道办事处不法人员告发，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日被安宁市国保警察抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，被西山区法院判处<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>个月有期徒刑，倪会仙刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">聂广丰：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">上海闵行区法轮功学员。家住闵行区灯辉路银春小区。因信仰法轮功，一直遭受迫害。<a name="_Hlk52327192">聂广丰</a><span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日被颛桥派出所警察抓捕、抄家，于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日被奉贤法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">聂丽娜</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">：，河南许昌市襄城县茨沟乡维权人士、访民。聂丽娜因投诉乡政府书记乔亚强，非法霸占其农耕地，进京维权十多年，不但诉求未得到落实，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年农历新年前夕，她母亲黄妙云的房子也被强拆。今年两会期间，聂丽娜带着八十多岁的老母亲到北京上访，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日再被刑事拘留。聂丽娜的一位要求匿名的亲友告诉本台，聂丽娜于已被刑事拘留。聂丽娜的母亲黄妙云则被公安警告，不得再到北京上访。，聂丽娜八旬母亲的房屋遭到数十人强拆。农历新年期间，她一家人惟有在寒冷中风餐露宿，大年除夕夜，她全家三口在篝火旁，吃着馒头就着咸菜过年，十分凄惨。聂丽娜被控“寻衅滋事罪”一案在<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日获判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US"> 3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">宁惠荣：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">男，满族人，基督徒，出生于<span lang="EN-US">1946</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月，原籍北京市，<span lang="EN-US">1966</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月赴新疆“支边”，供职于新疆哈密地区盐化工厂。<span lang="EN-US">2003</span>年，因抗议警察滥权的行为，走上维权之路。<span lang="EN-US">2007</span>年开始赴北京投诉。<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月，向北京市治安总队提交“游行示威”的申请报告，被指控“寻衅滋事”，遭到逮捕。<span lang="EN-US">2010</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月，被新疆地方当局判处三年半监禁，在新疆吐鲁番监狱服刑，因拒不认罪，未获减刑，<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月刑满出狱。宁惠荣于<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日在永定门长途汽车站，被劫访人员从<span lang="EN-US">102</span>路电车上劫走，<span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日被强行带回哈密后，被关押在哈密市公安局派出所，平板电脑、手机、钱包被扣押。宁惠荣因对哈密法院的枉法判决，在向最高人民法院申诉。他们就先抓人，再找罪名，关押至<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日下午，宁惠荣被送到哈密市医院，以治病的名义继续关押，白天二个人看守夜间三个人看守，人身自由被非法限制，至今仍被非法拘禁。后音信全无。</span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">牛占华：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">沈阳市法库县法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日<span lang="EN-US">0</span>时许，秀水河子镇派出所警察没有法定手续，擅自闯入牛占华家，翻箱倒柜，非法搜查，还带走牛占华和在牛占华家做客的周建国。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，牛占华在辽宁省沈阳市法库县法院被庭审。整个庭审现场被律师有理有据的辩护所主导，法官与公诉人大部份时间是听律师在讲，公诉人只是照本宣科的读了《起诉书》。最后律师要求法院应当立即释放牛占华。后于<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月对他判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">努尔哈因﹒木哈麦提沙尔（哈萨克）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">新疆伊利市哈萨克自治州阿尔泰市人，<span lang="EN-US">60</span>岁左右，哈萨克族，穆斯林。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">-8</span>月，中共新疆伊犁哈萨克自治州当局判处了一批穆斯林仪式祷告者，指控其因非法从事了穆斯林式常规祷告仪式，涉嫌法宗教活动或极端宗教活动。其中，努尔哈因﹒木哈麦提沙尔因在家里存有《古兰经》，被警方搜出，随被抓捕，现已被哈萨克自治州法院以“从事极端宗教活动”等为由秘密判刑<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">努尔兰：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">全名是哈德力别克·努尔兰。<span lang="EN-US">1990</span>年代出生，新疆维吾尔自治区阿尔泰地区青河县查干郭勒乡人，哈萨克斯坦族，穆斯林，乌鲁木齐市酷巴巴网络科技有限公司创办人，企业家，中国在押良心犯。早期曾就读于东北大学，<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年毕业；<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年，曾前往新疆乌鲁木齐市创业，后创办酷巴巴网络科技有限公司；<span lang="EN-US"> 2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，曾因宗教信仰而做礼拜（即穆斯林进行敬拜时的祷告方式），被阿尔泰地区青河县当局很快知晓，随被青河县警方带走拘留，并被送进“再教育营”进行洗脑式教育，自此失联；因其在“再教育营”拒绝接受洗脑教育，遂被警方以“从事非法宗教活动”为罪由转为正式逮捕；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月，被新疆维吾尔自治区阿尔泰地区青河县法院重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2028</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月； 据悉，其被判刑前后，家属均未收到任何法律文书，家属欲为其聘请辩护律师遭拒，探视权被剥夺，至今不让会面。目前在新疆克拉玛依市监狱服刑。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 22.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">O</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 22.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">．<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">欧彪峰、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">欧道齐、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">欧彪峰：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">湖南公民，民主维权人士。湖南公民欧彪峰因发帖声援董瑶琼，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日被湖南株洲国保传唤，<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日被行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">15</span>天。到期后又被以涉嫌颠覆国家主权罪指定居所监视居住了。近年来，欧彪峰积极参与公民维权活动，经常发布被政府打压的公民行动者的第<span lang="EN-US">1</span>手信息。今年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月及<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月，欧彪峰曾因为公开声援许志永和常玮平等良心犯被警方传唤。欧彪峰公开声援香港反送中社会运动，并在黎智英被抓捕后，公开表态支持黎智英及香港《苹果日报》。而有关方面曾多次透露早已做好了抓捕欧彪峰的材料。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">欧道齐：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">湖南省怀化市沅陵县官庄镇人，现居长沙开办少儿培训中心。年约<span lang="EN-US">40</span>岁。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>、<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日间被警方带走，罪名为“寻衅滋事”。欧道齐在长沙的培训机构与铺面也被查封。知情人说，<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，欧道齐所在的怀化地区老乡群中一网名为“糟老头子”的网友在聊天过程中以一句“习近平上台搞什么都犯法”，来表达对现实社会风声鹤唳草木皆兵的统治手法不满，其后该名友遭到警方抓捕，并有知情群员将警方的核查通报上传至该群组。随后多名网友将该图片转发到其他社交平台，其中就包括欧道齐。据称欧道齐将图片上传发布在推特后不久便被警方发现，并根据<span lang="EN-US">IP</span>地址将其拘捕。后音信全无。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 22.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">P</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">．<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">潘斌、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">潘培德</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、潘荣卿、潘彤、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">潘玉峰</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">庞永刚</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">兀亚莉、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">彭石清、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">彭文缄、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">彭宇华、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">朴顺南（朝鲜族）、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">普化（藏）、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">卜宝玲、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">潘斌：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1981</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日出生，重庆市涪陵区礁石镇人，复员军人，民主维权公民，中国在押维权人士。<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年，曾因要自己组建一个党，在网吧发信息时被警方抓捕，然后被重庆市公安局处劳动教养<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年；获释后，因致力于帮助良心犯和维权访民，随遭重庆当局严控打压，多次被喝茶、被旅游等；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，曾被重庆九龙坡区拆迁办及重庆九龙坡公安分局、石桥铺派出所警方暴力冲门，遭辱骂威胁，非法扣押身份证等，因长时不还身份证，致其奋而发声抗议声明；<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日，曾因声援重庆乐天事件而被警方强制旅游<span lang="EN-US">8</span>天；<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日，因组织当地维权访民集体上访，遂被重庆市涪陵区警方抓走，并被以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”刑拘；之后<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日被重庆市涪陵区检察院以同罪由转正式批捕，指控其因组织策划访民非法上访，冲击国家机关，涉嫌多次寻衅滋事，所以触犯了国家相关法律；据悉，关押期间，其曾被送精神病医院做强制性检查。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US"> 10</span>月<span lang="EN-US"> 9</span>日前一直被羁押于重庆市涪陵区蒿子坝看守所。潘斌涉嫌寻衅滋事案于<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日上午<span lang="EN-US">9</span>点半在重庆市涪陵法院开庭审理。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日被中共涪陵区人民法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">潘培德：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1956</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年生，退休工人，广东省茂名市电白区法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日下午<span lang="EN-US">4</span>点左右，潘培德在电白水东家里，警察对潘培德实施抓捕、抄家；下午<span lang="EN-US">6</span>点左右，又把他关押到米粮村老家抄家； 第<span lang="EN-US">2</span>天，即<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日下午，潘培德被刑事拘留。并被关押到茂名市第<span lang="EN-US">1</span>看守所关押。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日被茂名市茂南区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">潘荣卿：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">2017</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，山东省烟台市莱山区公安分局跨区出动大量警力，将一群手无寸铁的老太太绑架。这群人中<span lang="EN-US">70</span>岁以上的就有四位（<span lang="EN-US">79</span>岁的吴香仃，<span lang="EN-US">74</span>岁的张慧英，<span lang="EN-US">71</span>岁的韩忠香，<span lang="EN-US">70</span>岁的肖淑娴）；<span lang="EN-US">60</span>岁以上的也有四位（<span lang="EN-US">67</span>岁的邹本珍，<span lang="EN-US">65</span>岁的李爱茹，<span lang="EN-US">63</span>岁的马玉珍，<span lang="EN-US">63</span>岁的孙明秋），除此之外，还有赵淑玉，潘荣卿，潘艳岩，栾景尧（潘艳岩的丈夫），崔德英（另案处理）等人。目前，潘荣卿、潘艳岩、马玉珍、赵淑玉被关押于条件恶劣的烟台市福山看守所；韩忠香、肖淑娴、吴香仃、孙明秋、邹本珍被取保候审于原籍；张慧英现被监视居住于家中。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，莱山区检察院罔顾法律、事实，将上面十名无辜法轮功学员构陷到烟台市莱山区法院。后获悉，马玉珍被非法判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年，罚款<span lang="EN-US">4000</span>元；潘艳岩被非法判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，罚款<span lang="EN-US">7000</span>元；潘荣卿被非法判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，罚款<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 351.75pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">潘彤：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">内蒙古通辽维权人士，因维权释放多次遭当地警方行政拘留。其访民朋友杜红于<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日被通辽警方抓捕后，潘彤持续发声呼吁，自己因此于<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日被抓捕，随后遭刑事拘留，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年以寻衅滋事罪被重判<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。当局对潘彤指控的罪状就是所谓潘彤在网络上揭露了通辽当局的虚假信息而“引发大量网民对政府及司法机关公信力的质疑”。因此构成寻衅滋事罪，将潘彤判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">潘玉峰：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">辽宁朝阳市两法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日下午，潘玉峰在家中被北塔分局警察抓捕。潘玉峰是位难得的孝子，家中老母亲患老年痴呆，生活不能自理，一直由潘玉峰照顾。自潘玉峰被绑架后，老人无人照顾，很快消瘦了很多，在潘玉峰绑架近一年后老人悲苦离开人世，临终都未见到儿子一面。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，潘玉峰案开庭，律师做无罪辩护。后得知潘玉峰被双塔法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">庞永刚：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">男，<span lang="EN-US">1976</span>年生，河南许昌市魏都区七里店乡庞庄村民，退伍军人、法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月中旬，<a name="_Hlk52326633">庞永刚</a>从外面打工回来被抓捕抄家，被关押到许昌市看守所。后许昌市魏都区检察院对庞永刚起诉。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月被魏都区法院开庭，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年底被判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">兀亚莉：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">女，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年五十七岁，一九九九年四月开始修炼法轮功。曾被非法抄家五次、拘留四次、被洗脑班拘禁一次、劳教两年，<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日被绑架、冤判<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，长期被监视居住，遭受非法开除公职等迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月上旬，兀亚莉被汉中市汉台区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">彭石清：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">湖南省湘潭市人，湘潭市岳塘区板塘花苑居民小区居民，某工厂木工，法轮功信仰者，良心犯。因笃信法轮功而曾被当局多次抓捕关押，甚至曾被枉判<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年，并先后在沅江赤山监狱、常德津市监狱服刑，备受酷刑虐待。出狱后，因其依然坚持信仰不变，遂遭当局更严厉监控打压。<a name="_Hlk512558029"><span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日</a>早，突然被湘潭市公安高新分局双马派出所警方数十人闯入家中，将其夫妇二人双双抓走，随后家被查抄，搜走相关法轮功资料数份，并将其所有存折、银行卡、社保卡、身份证等私人物品也一并搜走。当日其即被送往湘潭市看守所关押。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，其妻熊春霞在被索要了<span lang="EN-US">3000</span>元保释金后准予释放回家，而其竟被以涉邪教罪转正式批捕，被指控因制作和发放法轮功真相资料、印制有法轮功真相内容的人民币，以及发送法轮功真相内容短信等，因此违反了相关法律。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日，其案在看守所内被湘潭市岳塘区法院秘密开庭，最终其被一审以“组织、利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年。目前被关押在湘潭市看守所。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">彭文缄：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">广东揭阳市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">1960</span>年代生人。家住揭阳市东阳办事处东山村。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日下午，揭阳市榕城区公安分局国保大队伙同揭阳市东阳派出所，到黄建民家进行抓捕抄家。因黄建民在自己家开了商店，经常收到一些真相币，此次抄家抄到了真相币，就成了国保抓捕黄建民的冠冕堂皇的借口了。后黄建民彭文缄夫妇被关押揭阳市看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，黄建民被判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年、妻子<a name="_Hlk52325427">彭文缄</a>被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">.</span>刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">彭宇华：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">1980</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日出生，湖北省籍人，理财经理，人权活动者。自<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年以来，因其创建了“两岸牵手”、“围观中国”、“围观华南”等系列<span lang="EN-US">QQ</span>群，并与李明哲等数十名境内外非政府组织成员及人权活动者，成立了旨在建立新型民主制度和进行中国大陆人权活动的“梅花公司”，遂被中共警方跟踪、监控。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日被湖南省长沙市国家安全局以涉嫌“颠覆国家政权罪”刑事拘留；同年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日，被长沙市检察院以同罪名正式批捕，同日被长沙市警方正式逮捕，并指控其创建了系列<span lang="EN-US">QQ</span>群，炒作近年来大陆发生的热点事件，发布诋毁、攻击政府部门和大陆制度的言论，成立了“旨在颠覆大陆政权、推翻大陆基本政治制度的组织<span lang="EN-US">'</span>梅花公司<span lang="EN-US">'</span>”，制定了组织纲领，确定了组织框架和人员细致分工，组织<span lang="EN-US">100</span>万成员插手围观所谓热点事件，触犯了中国法律。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日其案在岳阳市中级法院开庭受审，同年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日被该法院以“颠覆国家政权罪”判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年，剥权<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年。对于一审他表示服从判决。目前被羁押于湖南省岳阳市看守所。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">朴顺南（朝鲜）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1962</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日出生，辽宁省辽阳市人，朝鲜族，辽阳市朝光村基督教家庭教会负责人，中国在押良心犯。因其教会为基督教家庭教会，且不愿到中共当局指定的“三自”教会敬拜、聚会，遂遭致当局的严打惩罚；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，其被辽阳市太子河区警方突然以涉嫌“非法经营罪”抓捕刑拘，并被指控教会内部使用了基督徒信仰灵修崇拜书籍及相关印刷品，并在教会的便利店销往其他省市，属于非法买卖行为；同年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日被转正式逮捕；<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日被辽宁省辽阳市太子河区法院以“非法经营罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年。目前被羁押于辽阳市看守所。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">普化（藏）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">青海省黄南州同仁县多哇乡人，藏族人权捍卫者。<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月，中共<span lang="EN-US">18</span>大召开前夕、期间及之后，在藏区多地仅一个月内共发生了<span lang="EN-US">28</span>起自焚事件，当时同仁县就有<span lang="EN-US">9</span>位藏人自焚，其中多哇乡<span lang="EN-US">5</span>人自焚，均身亡。事发后，中共当局很快成立了青海省公安厅驻黄南州系列自焚案件专案组，并以涉嫌“散布自焚者照片并在照片上写下自焚者遗言”、“参与反政府示威抗议活动”等罪，抓捕藏民<span lang="EN-US">70</span>人。之后，有<span lang="EN-US">52</span>人被刑拘，有<span lang="EN-US">12</span>人被逮捕，普化即是其中宣布被正式逮捕者之一。<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，其多人在黄南州同仁县法院被宣判，普化被以不知名罪名重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">13</span>年。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">卜宝玲：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">女、<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">70</span>岁，黑龙江哈尔滨法轮功学员。哈尔滨市哈尔滨市依兰县公安局<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日下午对依兰县、佳木斯市桦川县两地法轮功学员实施绑架，到<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日共有<span lang="EN-US">29</span>人被绑架，其中十四名法轮功学员宋玉芝、施凤香、施凤兰、王云杰、周妍、邓术梅、宋孔华、武桂琴、卜宝玲、夏桂华、唐立飞、姚怀英、康艳玲、庞秀贤，与薛宏亮（未修炼法轮功）被长期关押构陷，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日遭依兰县法院庭审。卜宝玲被判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，处罚金<span lang="EN-US">3</span>万元，刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 22.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">Q</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">． <span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">恰特合•达吾列提（哈）、</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">钱风林、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">钱有云</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">强巴格勒（藏）、强巴旺秋（藏）、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">乔华荣、<span style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">乔莲红</span>、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">乔娜然、乔向阳、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">秦来宾、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">秦莲玉</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、秦艳秋、秦永敏、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">秦真</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">覃德富、覃永沛、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">邱汉浓、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">全世欣、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">曲红、曲嘉唯色（藏）、曲桑嘉措（藏）。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">恰特合·达吾列提（哈）：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1988</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日出生，新疆维吾尔自治区伊犁哈萨克斯坦自治州人，伊犁哈萨克斯坦自治州察布查尔锡伯自治县捷仁布拉克镇<span lang="EN-US">67</span>团<span lang="EN-US">8</span>连哈萨克族公民，中国在押良心犯。被抓捕前，一直是遵纪守法的好公民，并因身有严重疾患长期与病魔做着殊死搏斗；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，曾被新疆建设兵团农四师医院诊断为慢性粒细胞白血病；后因病情严重，于<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日被转到新疆医科大学第一附属医院住院治疗<span lang="EN-US">8</span>天；<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年，曾两度前往北京市住院治疗，但又因无力承担高昂的治疗费用<span lang="EN-US">,</span>只能中途放弃治疗；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，其病情再次复发，不得不在新疆医科大学第一附属医院住院治疗，每月药费<span lang="EN-US">3</span>万元；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日，恰特合·达吾列提被伊犁州察布查尔锡伯自治县警方突然以不明罪由抓捕，被送入当地“教育培训中心”（又称“再教育营”）接受中共洗脑式教育；同年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，旋即被察布查尔锡伯自治县检察院予以批捕；<span lang="EN-US"> 2019</span>年，被伊犁哈萨克斯坦自治州察布查尔锡伯自治县法院以不明罪名重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">19</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2037</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日； 据悉，其被判刑前因身患白血病严重，医生建议做干细胞移植手术，但向狱方申请保外就医以求手术治疗，遭拒；又悉，因其被抓捕判刑，其家人（妻子、两个孩子及其母亲）生活陷入困境。 目前疑似在新疆伊犁哈萨克斯坦自治州新源监狱服刑。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">钱风林：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">张家口法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日，钱风林女士在康保县县城张文营街上送法轮功台历时，遭国保大队吕正带人抓捕，<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日上午，遭庭审。<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日，钱风林被康保县法院一审判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，并处罚金一万元。钱风林不服判决，上诉到张家口中级法院。上诉被驳回。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">钱有云：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1964</span>年生于武汉市洪山区，原武汉市江夏区粮食局饲料公司职工。钱有云<span lang="EN-US">1998</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月开始修炼法轮功。因为信仰法轮大法，曾遭中共判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，<a name="_Hlk52326718">钱有云</a>和孙足英结伴在江夏区体育馆向人讲法轮功真相，被江夏区纸坊派出所抓捕，后被关押在武汉市东西湖第一女子看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月，钱有云和孙足英被武汉市洪山区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">强巴格勒</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">（藏）</span></b><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">四川省甘孜藏族羌族自治区州阿坝县尼措寺僧人，<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">23</span>岁，是道孚县人。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日傍晚<span lang="EN-US">8</span>点多钟，强巴格勒在前往附近一佛塔转经途中，突然被中共公安人员拘捕。被指在僧舍中挂有西藏国旗，并曾表露想要为西藏政教事业而自焚的念头。后音信全无。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">强巴旺秋（藏）</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">:1959</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年出生，西藏自治区边波隆都县索托乡（注：此为藏语拼音名，汉语地名不明，疑为拉萨市附近某县<span lang="EN-US">/</span>乡）人，藏名<span lang="EN-US">Jampel Wangchuk</span>，俗名次培（<span lang="EN-US">Tsephel</span>），拉萨市哲蚌寺洛色林僧院高级僧人、纪律纠察僧官，学者僧侣，中国在押良心犯。自幼成为僧侣，并在西藏拉萨市哲蚌寺所在僧侣学院进修学习；后因长期师从藏族著名佛学教师兰林仁波切（<span lang="EN-US">Lamrim<span style="mso-spacerun: yes;">&nbsp; </span>Rinpoche</span>），成为其身边主要弟子，随拥有深厚博学的藏传佛学知识，且被哲蚌寺洛色林僧院确定为高级僧人及纪律纠察僧官；<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月，西藏发生大规模以僧侣为主体的抗议示威活动，以表达对中共当局长期压制、管控藏区人民的不满；他们强烈呼吁中共当局要实现（或兑现）藏民族“自治独立”，并要求让达赖喇嘛回国返乡，对藏区进行自治管理等政治诉求；针对此，同年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，拉萨的哲蚌寺约有<span lang="EN-US">350</span>名僧侣亦本着推动实现这些诉求，发起进一步的大规模抗议活动，使事态迅速波及到整个拉萨市区，甚至四川及青海藏区；对于此次抗议行动，中共警方随即采取了制止行为，但又因中共手段过于极端，导致双方发生对峙冲突，期间部分僧人被抓；<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日，其被拉萨市警方突然以涉嫌“抗议活动”刑拘，自此失联；另有同寺僧侣好友贡觉尼玛、阿旺觉尼亦被拘捕；后其被拉萨市警方正式逮捕，理由是虽未参加当时的抗议示威，但因未能阻止所在寺庙僧人举行大规模抗议行动，遂属于违规或违反相关管理条例行为；<span lang="EN-US">2010</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月，在超期关押<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年之久后，终被拉萨市中级法院秘密重判无期徒刑，罪名不详；据悉，其辩护权遭剥夺，至今其在狱中健康状况及所处具体环境等均无下落。目前疑似在拉萨曲水监狱服刑。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">乔华荣<span lang="EN-US">:</span></span></b><a name="_Hlk54972303"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">乔华荣</span></a><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">、赵根法、黄春玲、刘洪兰四人都是山东省曲阜市的法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日，黄春玲在刘洪兰家做客，赵根法、乔华荣夫妻去看她们，刚坐下还没说几句话，曲阜市国保大队人员就进入刘洪兰家，以「非法集会、集体学法」等罪名，将他们抓捕至书院派出所，另外以「把你的包拿过来看一下」为由将赵根法钥匙夺走，在赵根法、乔华荣夫妻二人都不在场、家中无人的情况下抄家，将法轮功书籍、手机、光盘、笔记本计算机、内存卡、</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">U</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">盘等几十件物品劫走。第二天，即<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，赵根法被关押在曲阜市拘留所；乔华荣、刘洪兰被送往济宁市看守所进行关押；黄春玲被关押在泗水县拘留所。后赵根法、黄春玲、刘洪兰、乔华荣，被抓捕、关押一年多，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日遭济宁市任城区法院庭审，赵根法被判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年半，黄春玲、刘洪兰被判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个月，乔华荣被判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。四人都被非法罚款一万元。乔华荣刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">乔莲红：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">广州<span lang="EN-US">11.12</span>大抓捕被抓人员。广州国安局以颠覆国家政权为由，于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日在广州对民运人士进行了大抓捕，目前已有四人被抓捕，分别是：范一平、范文成、赖见君、乔莲红。被抓后，即遭指定监视居住，罪名是颠覆国家政权。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">乔娜然：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">河北省衡水市安平县法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日下午，乔娜然遭到安平县公安绑架，被关押到衡水看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日得知，乔娜然被安平县法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">乔向阳：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">河南新郑市法轮功信徒、残疾人。家住新郑市龙湖镇沙窝李村，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日下午被新郑市警方以“扫黑除恶”的名义抓捕，家中私人物品被掠走。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，新郑市法院对乔向阳判刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">秦来宾：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">河南商丘网友，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日傍晚被警方约谈，<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日被控涉嫌寻衅滋事刑事拘留，羁押在商丘市看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日遭正式逮捕，其家人透露被捕原因是在推特发贴攻击国家领导人。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日被商丘市睢阳区法院以寻衅滋事罪由判处<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年有期徒刑，<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日转送周口西华监狱服刑，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">秦莲玉：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">浙江宁波市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，宁波市二十多名法轮功学员被当局绑架，遭受不同程度的迫害，<a name="_Hlk52326279">秦莲玉</a>被关押在宁波市看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日，在宁波市镇海区法院，秦莲玉案第二次被开庭，其被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，罚款六千元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">秦艳秋<span lang="EN-US">:</span></span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"> </span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">江苏省太仓市法轮功学员。原是苏州太仓邮政局职员，曾经<span lang="EN-US">6</span>次被绑架迫害，被劳教<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个月，被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，并被关过精神病院六个月迫害。她丈夫石泽惠曾<span lang="EN-US">7</span>次被绑架，被劳教<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，被判刑两次共<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年半。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，秦艳秋被太仓<span lang="EN-US">610</span>国保警察绑架。同时被绑架的法轮功学员还有董美英与陈永林。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">秦艳秋、董美英<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">秦永敏：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">1953</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日出生，湖北省鄂州市籍人，早年为湖北省武汉钢铁公司冷轧厂职工，著名民间政治学者、自由撰稿人，中国民主党湖北省党部重要创始人，“中国人权观察”（注册中）理事长、“玫瑰中国团队”负责人，著名人权活动家，中国在押政治犯。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，其被湖北省当局再度非法抓捕，罪由是“接受外媒采访及写文章过多”，其妻亦遭当局拘押、失联；<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日获悉，其已被湖北省武汉市警方以涉嫌“煽动颠覆国家政权罪”秘密羁押。现得知被羁押于武汉市第二看守所，案子在检察院。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日第一次获律师会见，状态良好。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">2018</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日上午在武汉中级法院三号审判庭公开宣判。秦永敏被以颠覆政权罪判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">13</span>年，剥夺政治权利<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。刑期自<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日起至<span lang="EN-US">2028</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日止。</span><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">秦真：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">耿潇男丈夫。因妻子大胆言论而被株连。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，秦真<span lang="EN-US">/</span>耿潇男夫妇二人突然被警方带走，随后被北京市海淀区警方以涉嫌”非法经营罪“刑拘，现在北京市海淀区看守所关押；北京当局曾以经济问题为名调查其二人所属的出版公司，秦真与公司的账号均被查封；多名好友均称其被抓捕，与此前其妻子耿潇男公开为多名中国公共知识分子及异见人士发声呼吁有关，乃是因妻子言遭株连。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月遭正式逮捕。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">覃德富：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">四川省人，基督徒，成都秋雨圣约归正家庭教会长老，<span lang="EN-US">12</span>·<span lang="EN-US">9</span>成都秋雨教案当事人之一，中国在押良心犯。近年来受洗皈依基督教，后在成都秋雨圣约家庭教会当长老；因与牧师王怡等众神职人员及信徒多次在成都市街头宣传基督教福音，并坚持其所在教会以“家庭教会”模式为主聚会，拒绝参加中共认可的“三自教会”，遂遭中共当局严酷打压；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，其在<span lang="EN-US">12</span>·<span lang="EN-US">9</span>秋雨教案大抓捕中被成都市青羊区警方以涉嫌“非法经营罪”刑拘；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，被以“非法经营罪”判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体;
