font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">宋孔华：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">男、<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">58</span>岁，黑龙江哈尔滨法轮功学员。哈尔滨市哈尔滨市依兰县公安局<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日下午对依兰县、佳木斯市桦川县两地法轮功学员实施绑架，到<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日共有<span lang="EN-US">29</span>人被绑架，其中十四名法轮功学员宋玉芝、施凤香、施凤兰、王云杰、周妍、邓术梅、宋孔华、武桂琴、卜宝玲、夏桂华、唐立飞、姚怀英、康艳玲、庞秀贤，与薛宏亮（未修炼法轮功）被长期关押构陷，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日遭依兰县法院庭审。宋孔华被判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年， 处罚金<span lang="EN-US">3</span>万元，刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">宋玉洁：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">辽宁省丹东市访民。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日晚上，辽宁省辽阳市访民王静和辽宁省丹东市访民宋玉洁，在北京市大兴区六合庄住处被辖区大兴分局北臧村派出所抓捕，送交地方公安接回，王静被辽阳带回后平安回家，而宋玉洁被丹东带回后被关进看守所。此前，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日凌晨零点<span lang="EN-US">40</span>分，辽宁省丹东市驻京维稳人员<span lang="EN-US">10</span>余人，闯入张正廷、宋玉洁夫妇俩位于北京市大兴区的暂住地，这些人强行将<span lang="EN-US">76</span>岁的张正廷截回辽宁丹东，以涉嫌“敲诈勒索罪”刑事拘留。张正廷的爱人宋玉洁说，地方政府之所以截人，是因为自己拒绝接受政府提出的给予<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万元人民币的维稳补助费，要求在“六四”敏感日前回丹东所致。到<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，张正廷被以“涉嫌寻衅滋事罪”批准逮捕。后音信全无。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">宋玉芝：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">女、<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">65</span>岁，黑龙江哈尔滨法轮功学员。哈尔滨市哈尔滨市依兰县公安局<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日下午对依兰县、佳木斯市桦川县两地法轮功学员实施绑架，到<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日共有<span lang="EN-US">29</span>人被绑架，其中十四名法轮功学员宋玉芝、施凤香、施凤兰、王云杰、周妍、邓术梅、宋孔华、武桂琴、卜宝玲、夏桂华、唐立飞、姚怀英、康艳玲、庞秀贤，与薛宏亮（未修炼法轮功）被长期关押构陷，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日遭依兰县法院庭审。宋玉芝被判刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年， 处罚金<span lang="EN-US">6</span>万<span lang="EN-US">5</span>千元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">宋志刚：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">辽宁省葫芦岛市兴城市人，兴城市农机修造厂职工，法轮功信仰者，良心犯。因手机丢失，被他人拾到后送到公安局，公安局发现他的手机中存有与法轮功有关的内容，随于<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日被新疆阿克陶县公安局拘捕，后被阿克陶县检察院以涉嫌“利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”批捕，并被关押在阿克陶县看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月被新疆阿克陶县法院以同罪名枉法重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">14</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2031</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">苏东亮</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">：<span lang="EN-US">1981</span>年出生，前陕西省府谷县法院书记员、民事审判第一庭助审员，维权公民，新公民运动参与者。<span lang="EN-US">2007</span>年毕业于西北政法大学之后，<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年，在陕西省府谷县法院参加工作并任书记员；<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年，任民事审判第一庭助理审判员，此期间，一直对现行司法体系的混乱与腐败等问题感到悲凉和无奈，并积极寻求如何改变社会问题的民主之路；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年初，他毅然辞去原有工作，前往广州等地参加民主活动，并与张六毛、项逢选等人结为好友，经常参与围观声援、同城聚餐等活动；<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日与张六毛、项逢选等多人一同被广州市珠海区警方以涉“颠覆国家政权罪”刑拘。一个月后被广州天河区检察院以涉“危害国家安全罪”正式批捕，并被定性为“制造炸弹危害公共安全案”主犯之一；<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日，获悉与其同案的维权公民张六毛在广州第三看守所被酷刑致死，而依然毫无信息，其家人亦因受官方恐吓而拒绝与外界联系。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月得知，其可能已与项逢选一起被广州市中级法院以“危害国家安全案主犯”判刑。目前服刑监狱不详。刑期不详。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">苏坤：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">60</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">多岁，黑龙江省哈尔滨市尚志市苇河镇人，法轮功学员。因信法轮功而屡遭中共<span lang="EN-US">610</span>办公室严厉逼迫打击。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，当二人与法轮功学员革振华一起坐着微型面包车去哈尔滨市尚志市亮河镇挂条幅、散发法轮功宣传资料时，被恶人告发，回来的路上在亚布力镇，被赶来的当地警方围堵抓捕，前挡风玻璃被打碎，车辆被扣押，次日即被警方以涉邪教罪刑事拘留。同年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日二人被转正式逮捕，同时关押在哈尔滨市第二看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，其案件被尚志市检察院向尚志市法院提起诉讼，并提出对革振华、苏坤冤判<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">-6</span>年，对王翠娥冤判<span lang="EN-US">2-3</span>年的建议。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日，二人被哈尔滨市尚志市法院以“利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”分别枉法重判：苏坤被判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年、罚金<span lang="EN-US">4</span>万，王翠娥被判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年、罚金<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万。二人不服，提起上诉。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，经哈尔滨市中级法院二审重新改判：苏坤被判<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年、罚金<span lang="EN-US">2</span>万，王翠娥被判<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年、罚金<span lang="EN-US">5</span>千。据悉，关押期间，整整有半年时间，其家人均无任何他们的消息，知道后也不许家里人接见、只叫存钱，不许带进物品，庭审也没有通知家属。最终，<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">苏坤刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，</b>王翠娥刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">宿慧娜：女，</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">辽宁省丹东市人，法轮功学员。在北京工作，居住在北京市昌平区沙河镇。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，宿慧娜贴法轮功传单，被监控录像看到后，被跟踪抓捕到北京市朝阳分局大屯派出所。警察在她包里翻出法轮功粘贴，随后对她抄家。宿慧娜后被关押到北京市朝阳看守所。宿慧娜被抓捕、关押在北京市朝阳看守所<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年多，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月被北京朝阳区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">隋永彦</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：<span lang="EN-US">1950</span>年代生人，辽宁丹东法轮功学员，原建筑造价工程师。面对中共对法轮功迫害，隋永彦曾经<span lang="EN-US">3</span>次被丹东站前派出所警察抓捕、抄家，并被劳教、判刑。<span lang="EN-US">2000</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月，隋永彦遭抓捕、抄家后，被关进辽宁本溪教养院，遭劳教<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2004</span>年，警察到隋永彦的工作单位实施抓捕，他工作用的电脑也被抄走，并被抄家。<span lang="EN-US">2004</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日，隋永彦被关押在盘锦监狱迫害<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月，隋永彦又被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，被劫入本溪监狱迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日上午遭丹东市振安区珍珠路派出所警察监控、抓捕、构陷，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月末被判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">索南次帕（藏）</span></b><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">西藏昌都地区八宿县人，青年作家，曾在定日县经商。曾因持有达赖喇嘛尊者法像而两次入狱。<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年，索南次帕就曾被冠上“危害国家安全罪”而被判两年徒刑；<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月，他再次被当局指控“撰写煽动民族矛盾文章、散发达赖喇嘛法像、破坏社会稳定”等，在拉萨遭关押一个月左右，并被处以罚款。索南次帕于<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19&nbsp;</span>日在西藏首都拉萨再次遭当地公安拘捕，这是<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年以来第三次遭到中共公安的拘捕。目前亲友仍不清楚索南次帕被捕的原因，以及关押地点等情况。后音信全无。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">索南达夫（藏）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">出生年月不详，四川省甘孜藏族自治州炉霍县人，藏族，中国在押政治犯。因中共当局在西藏及其周边各省涉藏地区强硬推行“爱国和法制宣传教育”活动，不准挂达赖喇嘛头像等，引发多地藏民强烈不满；<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月，四川省甘孜州炉霍县僧俗藏人亦举行大规模和平示威游行，要求西藏自由，信仰自由，并高呼达赖喇嘛万岁等口号，随即遭到中共警方的武力镇压和大规模抓捕，警民冲突升级；最终导致多人被打死打伤，上百藏人在当时及随后被抓或失踪，数十人被当局判处<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>个月至无期徒刑不等的刑期；索南达夫本人也因积极参与抗议示威活动，被警方以“聚众闹事”、 “参与炉霍县抗议示威和严重影响公共秩序的非法聚集”以及与境外势力有染等为由抓走，后被甘孜藏族自治州炉霍县法院以同罪由重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年。目前服刑地点不详。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">索南公保（藏）：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">1985</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">年出生，四川省甘孜藏族自治州新吧龙县人，藏名<span lang="EN-US">Solnam Gonpo</span>，原甘孜藏族自治州新龙县塘吉乡（音译）小学厨师，藏族人权捍卫者。曾因积极参与罢耕运动和抵制中共控制的藏历新年庆祝活动，<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，被当局怀疑参与在该县塘吉乡（音译）境内的一起有关抗议中共暴政，散发传单、呼吁西藏独立的示威活动；事发当天因该抗议活动引发警民冲突，乡政府办公大楼发生火灾，<span lang="EN-US"> 2009</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日，随于被新龙县警方强行抓捕，并被以涉嫌“煽动分裂国家罪”和“扰乱社会秩序罪”刑事拘留，关押于四川省成都市某看守所；<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，被四川省甘孜州中级法院以“煽动分裂国家”和“扰乱社会秩序”两项罪名判处无期徒刑。目前在四川省德阳市黄许镇德阳监狱服刑。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">索南林珠（藏）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">四川甘孜藏区炉霍县人，藏族人权捍卫者。<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，在西藏康区炉霍县境内发生大规模和平示威活动后，中共军警釆取武力镇压，导致云丹为首的多名藏人被开枪打死或打伤，上百人遭捕。<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日中共当局对<span lang="EN-US">16</span>名遭捕的藏人进行判决，其中一名藏人被判终身监禁，另有多人遭<span lang="EN-US">1</span>至<span lang="EN-US">13</span>年不等的有期徒刑。这<span lang="EN-US">16</span>名被判藏人中，已确切得知的有<span lang="EN-US">10</span>名藏人具体情况，其中：索南林珠，<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">30</span>多岁，被判无期徒刑。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">孙大午：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1954</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月生，河北省徐水县高林村镇郎五庄村人，河北大午农牧集团有限公司董事长。 孙大午初中毕业后曾待过山西临汾二十八军八十二师与徐水县农行，这两个经历让他发现农牧业可以发展经营。<span lang="EN-US">1985</span>年他创立大午农牧集团有限公司，担任董事长，以一千只鸡与五十头猪起家。担任董事长期间，孙大午于<span lang="EN-US">1996</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月获颁河北省养鸡状元荣誉。<span lang="EN-US">1995</span>年，大午集团已经成为中国五百大私营企业之一，孙大午也获选为保定市人大代表。<span lang="EN-US">1996</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月，他当选保定市禽蛋产业联合会理事长。<span lang="EN-US">2001</span>年，孙大午除了大午集团董事长外，亦兼任大午学校校长；<span lang="EN-US">2002</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月，他被中国农业大学农民问题研究所聘请为高级研究员。<span lang="EN-US"> 2003</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日，徐水县公安局通知大午网站：该网站发表的《小康社会的建设及难点》《悼念李慎之》《两位民间商人关于中国的时局及历史的对话》三篇文章严重损害了国家机关的形象，整顿网站，停止营业<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，罚款<span lang="EN-US">15000</span>元。<span lang="EN-US"> 2003</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，他被指向三千多户农民借款达一亿八千多万元而被捕，并以非法集资的罪名遭到收押，并被指控其非法持有弹药；两位弟弟大午集团副董事长孙志华、总经理孙德华和集团的财务处长也都被扣留。 最终徐水县法院以非法吸收公众存款的罪名判其有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年、缓刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，罚金<span lang="EN-US">10</span>万元，大午集团同时也被判处罚金三十万元。于<span lang="EN-US">2003</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日出狱回家。孙大午于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日被河北高碑店市公安局刑事拘留，指控他涉嫌寻衅滋事罪和破坏生产经营。同时，其妻子、两个儿子儿媳、公司高管等<span lang="EN-US">28</span>人一并被抓捕。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">孙德香：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1956</span>年生，黑龙江省伊春市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，中共开始疯狂迫害法轮功，孙德香遭中共邪党人员抓捕、关押，<span lang="EN-US">2010</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日曾经被判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月初，孙德香被伊春市公安局恶警秘密抓捕。孙德香后被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，现已被劫入黑龙江省女子监狱。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月初。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">孙桂昌：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">吉林省德惠市五台乡法轮功学员。孙桂昌和肖永芬夫妇各被非法判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年，已经于<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月份被羁押到公主岭监狱和吉林省女子监狱。孙桂昌和妻子肖永芬<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日被不法警察入室绑架。孙贵昌被送到德惠市拘留所非法拘留五天。肖永芬被送到长春第二看守所检查身体，不合格拒收，第二天下午<span lang="EN-US">7</span>点多钟放回家，被监视居住。后来，孙桂昌被非法关押德惠看守所。肖永芬因身体和精神状况被放回家，并被监视居住。<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日左右，吉林省公安厅数个警察将在其女儿看家的肖永芬绑架。据悉，肖永芬以前在长春黑嘴子劳教所被迫害得精神失常，现在患有高血压和糖尿病（后期），脚部严重溃烂，现在被关押在吉林省女子监狱八监区；孙桂昌被关押在公主岭监狱九监区。多年来，上述两个监狱公开执法犯法，利用死人床、坐小板凳、长期剥夺睡眠、电棍电击、殴打、上绳等各种酷刑残害和转化善良无辜的法轮功学员，多人被迫害致伤、致残、致疯、致死。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">孙桂芳：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">大连市金州区法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1952</span>生。因修炼法轮功，<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年曾经被劳教<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年、在马三家劳动教养院遭受迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，大连市公安局金州分局国保和金州区拥政派出所，由金州区古城甲区社区主任王新配合诱骗说楼下漏水，闯入家中绑架孙桂芳和另两位法轮功学员，并非法抄家，抢走法轮功书籍若干以及大量私人物品。孙桂芳<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日被送大连市看守所关押，同年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日被批捕。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日，孙桂芳老人在大连市金州区法院被庭审，律师在法庭上为孙桂芳做了无罪辩护。后得知孙桂芳被大连市金州区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">孙建锋</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">：宁夏中卫市中宁县法轮功学员。自<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年中共对法轮功持续至今已逾二十多年的迫害中，<span lang="EN-US">1972</span>年生的孙建锋先生曾经被劳教<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年半、判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日晚，孙建锋先生被一小区的保安诬告，警察将孙建锋绑架后搜身，并闯入孙建锋家抄家，劫掠了两本大法书籍，随后将孙建锋劫持到中宁县看守所关押，后孙建锋被批捕。孙建锋先生<span lang="EN-US">2010</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日被判<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>个月。孙建锋已经被关押到宁夏石嘴山监狱服刑。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">孙金奎：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">黑龙江鸡西市鸡冠区法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日至<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，鸡西市鸡冠区十名法轮功学员遭黑龙江省公安、鸡西市警察绑架，二零二零年十月二十三日，孙金奎被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">孙俊：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">大连市中山区人，大连市热电公司职工，法轮功学员，良心犯。孙俊因是张霞的丈夫，<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日下班后发现家被抄，就到青云小学询问，才知妻子已被民主广场派出所警方抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，孙俊到民主广场派出所询问妻子情况时也被警方扣押，后送姚家看守所羁押。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，夫妇二人被中山区检察院以涉嫌“邪教罪”正式批捕，后被秘密开庭，最终被大连市中山区法院一审以“利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”判处<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>个月。其不服提起上诉，大连市中级法院未经二审开庭即对他维持原判。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月底，孙俊被送往大连市监狱服刑。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">孙平：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">山东省日照市法轮功学员，日照市裕华机械厂职工。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>、<span lang="EN-US">3</span>两日，日照市公安局东港分局国保警察先后抓捕了法轮功学员公华、孙平、屈正蓉等八位大法学员，关押在日照市看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日孙平被判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">孙润桃：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">河北省张家口市沽源县法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日下午，沽源县法轮功学员高清秀、孙润桃、赵梅在长梁乡顺路讲法轮功、免费传递法轮功法轮功资料时，遭人恶告，遭警方抓捕。孙润桃和高清秀<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日，分别被张北县法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年和<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，勒索罚款<span lang="EN-US">2</span>万元。孙润桃刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">孙茜：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">加拿大华裔女富商。孙茜是北京利德曼生物化学公司的创始人，<span lang="EN-US">2007</span>年获加拿大国籍，<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年和<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年登上胡润中国富豪榜，身家<span lang="EN-US">35</span>亿。由于操劳过度，身体严重透支，孙茜患上多种疾病，多方医治无效。在<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年她学习炼法轮功。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，孙茜正在家中与表妹聊天，警方突然闯入抄家，搜出法轮功相关书籍后，将她抓捕。期间，孙茜多次遭受酷刑，被铐在铁椅子上，被辣椒水喷脸。全天被戴上镣铐，强制洗脑，强迫放弃她的信仰。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，孙茜一案在北京朝阳法院温榆河法庭开庭，孙茜获刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">孙永耀：</span></b><a name="_Hlk52322719"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1970</span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk52322719;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日出生，安徽省阜南县人，阜南县鹿城镇刘寨村孙西组<span lang="EN-US">13</span>号公民，基督徒，安徽省阜南县基督教堂主任牧师，中国在押良心犯。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月，其所在教会接到当地政府发来的要求拆除教堂通知，称其教堂因地处政府要进行街道棚改项目改造规划的范畴，故而必须拆除；由于地方当局仅对其所在教会提出单方面拆迁补偿方案，并称如要教堂异地重建，政府将不给予相应补偿；因此通告方案明显有失公允，立刻遭到其及教会众信徒的坚决反对，遂遭地方当局的恶意报复与打击；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，正当众信徒在教会举行聚会和敬拜时，突然被官方拆迁公司闯入，并在无任何合法档及拆除手续的情况下实施强拆，因事发突然，教会里面的所有物品均未及时搬出，终致所有财物几近损毁；因其坚决反对政府强拆教堂的举动，同年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，遂与教会主任耿宜敏等神职人员一同被阜南市警方抓捕，次日被以涉“聚众扰乱社会秩序罪”刑拘；<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk52322719;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">同年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，被阜阳县检察院予以批捕；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，其案在安徽省阜南县法院开庭受审；<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日，被该法院一审以“聚众扰乱社会秩序罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月；其不服，提起上诉；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，安徽省阜阳市中级法院经二审裁决，认为“原判认定的部分事实不清，证据不足”，故撤销原判，发回重审。目前被羁押于阜南县看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk52322719;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">孙占国</span></b></span><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">吉林省松原市干安县法轮功学员。家住松原市干安县唱子村，在中共对法轮功的疯狂迫害中，孙占国曾连续两次被非法劳教，曾被关押在吉林省九台饮马河劳教所，遭受酷刑虐待。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月被干安县油田采油厂派出所抓捕，被关押一年后，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月被干安县法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">孙志芬</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">：山西太原市老年法轮功学员。太原市公安局迎泽分局警察<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日非法闯民宅，抄家抓捕法轮功学员孙志芬（<span lang="EN-US">60</span>岁）、王素平（<span lang="EN-US">67</span>岁）、罗保军（<span lang="EN-US">62</span>岁）、张清香（<span lang="EN-US">69</span>岁）、张润英（<span lang="EN-US">71</span>岁）、郭润鲜（<span lang="EN-US">68</span>岁）、田玉琴（<span lang="EN-US">60</span>岁）、胡兰英（<span lang="EN-US">65</span>岁），其中多数是老太太。山西省太原市这八位老年法轮功学员被非法关押近一年后得知被迎泽区法院非法判刑、勒索罚款，并被劫持到监狱。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">被判刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年，罚金<span lang="EN-US">3</span>万元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2028</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">孙忠琴：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1952</span>年生，辽宁凤城法轮功学员。孙忠琴因为向民众讲清法轮功，<span lang="EN-US">2007</span>年，曾被马三家劳教所劳教<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年，期间受尽酷刑和奴役，<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，在辽宁女子监狱，被恶警指使犯人关进小黑屋里暴力殴打、扒光衣服浇凉水等。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，丹东市凤城市法轮功学员鞠世淼、孙忠琴、佟秀红，在凤城大兴镇，给村民送明慧新年台历、福字和期刊等，被大兴镇政法综治委员宋传刚等人抓捕，后被构陷到丹东市振安区法院。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，<span lang="EN-US">3</span>位法轮功学员被丹东市振安区法院判刑：鞠世淼被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，勒索罚款<span lang="EN-US">5</span>千元；孙忠琴<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，勒索罚款<span lang="EN-US">5</span>千元；佟秀红<span lang="EN-US">11</span>个月，勒索罚款<span lang="EN-US">3</span>千元。佟秀红于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日被“取保候审”，已回家。孙忠琴刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">孙足英：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1967</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日生，江夏区粮食加工米厂职工家属。因为信仰法轮大法，曾遭中共判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，钱有云和<a name="_Hlk52326798">孙足英</a>结伴在江夏区体育馆向人讲法轮功真相，被江夏区纸坊派出所抓捕，后被关押在武汉市东西湖第一女子看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月，钱有云和孙足英被武汉市洪山区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></b></p>
</div>
